                <li class="layout-content-panel content_background content_text_border grid-col grid-col-horiz grid-col-vert grid-col-12"><div class="layout-content-panel-container">
                            <div class="content-blog-title content-html content-font-l content-font-margin">
        How to support Indivisible</div>
                        
                            <div class="content-blog-details content-font-s content-font-margin content_text_alt">
        <a href="http://lightpinkdaytripper.tumblr.com/post/132587659954" target="_blank"> <span class="global-local-date" data-timestamp="1446705041">Nov 05, 15</span></a>
    </div>
                        
                        <div class="content-blog-body content-html content-font-m">
        <p><a class="tumblr_blog" href="http://lumaga.tumblr.com/post/132539276859">lumaga</a>:</p>
<blockquote>
<p><a class="tumblr_blog" href="http://spoofenshmirtz.tumblr.com/post/132144541981">spoofenshmirtz</a>:</p>
<blockquote>
<p><figure class="tmblr-full"><span data-src="http://41.media.tumblr.com/82c4194414c8deb2e79968b4317235e6/tumblr_inline_nwzewnusOF1qliee4_540.png" class="image-deferred"></span></figure></p><ul><li>
<b>Spread information about the game itself!</b> Many people (including myself) tend to focus on Lab Zero and their situation in relation to Indivisible, but it doesn’t tell people who don’t know who Lab Zero Games are or what Skullgirls is why funding Indivisible would be a good idea! Base your information on the prototype but remember to include that it’s not a finalized concept for the gameplay itself and that player input will be considered by LZ (and already has in the making of the prototype)!<br/></li>
<li>
<b>Play the prototype! Tell other people about the prototype!</b> Spread the prototype around and tell people about the love and care that went into the creation of just this prototype, give them accurate information regarding the making of it and how it’s NOT a demo or even perfectly representative of what the game will be if it’s funded! It’s something LZ wrapped together in three months just for the sake of promoting their product simply because they care so much about the game they want to make!</li>
<li>
<b>Draw fanart!!</b> Draw lots and lots of fanart! Let people see the characters LZ made and be vocal about your support of it! I know lots of people feel like it’s hopeless because of how much money they still need to be funded, but if you don’t shut up about it and keep promoting the game through art or videos or any other means, more people will hear about it!</li>
<li>
<b>Meet misconceptions with calmness!</b> When people are cynical towards the crowdfunding model, counter them with simple facts about LZ’s plans! Watch the videos where Mike Z himself gives informative information about what it takes to make a game (<a href="https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=8vddobPtDrE">here</a> and <a href="https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vvCOCgnBzjo">here</a>), and use this information in your arguments! Try not to guilt trip people, though; I can see how that could be counterproductive and ultimately work against the campaign itself.</li>
<li>Whenever you talk about Indivisible,<b> ALWAYS INCLUDE A LINK TO THE CAMPAIGN AND THE PROTOTYPE!</b> People need to know where to go to support the game! Make people WANT to support it, be positive and friendly!</li>
</ul><p>We’ve passed $500k, 1/3 of the fixed goal, and there’s a little over 2 weeks left to spread it around and convince people to fund it. If we continue to talk about the game positively and spread correct information about the game itself, <b>we can do this.</b> It’s not over until IGG says it’s over, and it’s not over for at least another 2 weeks.</p>
<p><a href="https://www.indiegogo.com/projects/indivisible-a-2d-rpg-for-ps4-xb1-win-mac-linux#/">Support Indivisible. Play the prototype. Be optimistic and positive.</a></p>
</blockquote>
<p>I worked for the prototype, and I’ll probably be working for the full game if it gets funded!<br/>Go check out the awesome characters that have been revealed so far, play the prototype, and spread the word~</p>
</blockquote></div>
                        

                    </div>

                </li>
